<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Why Setup Required?</h4><a id="user-content-why-setup-required" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why Setup Required?" href="#why-setup-required"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>🔒 Security by Design:</strong> Operating systems block direct system audio access for privacy protection - this is universal across all platforms and applications.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>⚙️ Quick Setup Process:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>macOS:</strong> Install BlackHole (free) + Audio MIDI Setup (5 min)</li>
<li><strong>Windows:</strong> Enable built-in Stereo Mix OR install VB-Cable (free) (3 min)</li>
<li><strong>Linux:</strong> Use built-in PulseAudio monitors (usually works out-of-box)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><a href="/iamsrikanthnani/pluely/blob/master/SYSTEM_AUDIO_SETUP.md">📖 Complete Audio Setup Guide</a></strong> • <strong>Step-by-step for all platforms</strong></p>

</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Additional STT Providers:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Groq Whisper</strong>: Add your Groq API key and select Whisper model</li>
<li><strong>Google Speech-to-Text</strong>: Add your Google API key for speech recognition</li>
<li><strong>Deepgram STT</strong>: Add your Deepgram API key and select model</li>
<li><strong>Azure Speech-to-Text</strong>: Add your Azure subscription key and configure region</li>
<li><strong>Speechmatics</strong>: Add your Speechmatics API key for transcription</li>
<li><strong>Rev.ai STT</strong>: Add your Rev.ai API key for speech-to-text</li>
<li><strong>IBM Watson STT</strong>: Add your IBM Watson API key and configure service</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🎙️ <strong>STT Provider Configuration</strong></h4><a id="user-content-️-stt-provider-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🎙️ STT Provider Configuration" href="#️-stt-provider-configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Each STT provider comes pre-configured with optimal settings:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>🎯 Real-time Processing</strong>: Instant speech recognition with voice activity detection</li>
<li><strong>🌍 Multi-Language Support</strong>: Choose providers optimized for specific languages</li>
<li><strong>⚡ Fast &amp; Accurate</strong>: Industry-leading transcription accuracy and speed</li>
<li><strong>🔒 Secure Authentication</strong>: API keys stored locally and securely</li>
<li><strong>🎨 Seamless Integration</strong>: Works with Pluely's voice input features</li>
<li><strong>🔧 Custom Variables</strong>: Support for dynamic variables in custom STT providers</li>
<li><strong>🌐 Any STT Provider</strong>: Full compatibility with any speech recognition API endpoint</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🛠️ <strong>Custom STT Provider Setup</strong></h4><a id="user-content-️-custom-stt-provider-setup" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🛠️ Custom STT Provider Setup" href="#️-custom-stt-provider-setup"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For STT providers not in our list, use the custom STT provider option with full control:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>🌐 Any Speech Recognition API</strong>: Add any STT provider with REST API support</li>
<li><strong>🔐 Flexible Authentication</strong>: Bearer tokens, API keys, custom headers, or direct key embedding</li>
<li><strong>📡 Response Path Mapping</strong>: Configure where to extract transcription text from any API response structure</li>
<li><strong>🔧 Dynamic Variables</strong>: Create custom variables using <code>{{VARIABLE_NAME}}</code> format in curl commands</li>
<li><strong>📝 Request Customization</strong>: Full control over headers, body structure, and parameters</li>
<li><strong>⚙️ Audio Format Support</strong>: Support for various audio formats and sample rates</li>
<li><strong>🔄 Real-Time Testing</strong>: Test your custom STT provider setup instantly</li>
</ul>

<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>🎯 The Ultimate Stealth AI Assistant - Invisible to Everyone</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Pluely is engineered to be <strong>completely invisible</strong> during your most sensitive moments:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>🔍 Undetectable in video calls</strong> - Works seamlessly in Zoom, Google Meet, Microsoft Teams, Slack Huddles, and all other meeting platforms</li>
<li><strong>📺 Invisible in screen shares</strong> - Your audience will never know you're using AI assistance</li>
<li><strong>📸 Screenshot-proof design</strong> - Extremely difficult to capture in screenshots due to translucent overlay</li>
<li><strong>🏢 Meeting room safe</strong> - Won't appear on projectors or shared screens</li>
<li><strong>🎥 Recording invisible</strong> - Doesn't show up in meeting recordings or live streams</li>
<li><strong>⚡ Instant hide/show</strong> - Overlaps with any window on your PC/Desktop for quick access</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Perfect for confidential scenarios where discretion is absolutely critical.</strong></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Blazingly Fast with Tauri</strong></h3><a id="user-content-blazingly-fast-with-tauri" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Blazingly Fast with Tauri" href="#blazingly-fast-with-tauri"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Built with <strong>Tauri</strong>, Pluely delivers native desktop performance with minimal resource usage:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Instant startup</strong> - launches in milliseconds</li>
<li><strong>10x smaller</strong> than Electron apps (~10MB vs ~100MB)</li>
<li><strong>Native performance</strong> - no browser overhead</li>
<li><strong>Memory efficient</strong> - uses 50% less RAM than web-based alternatives</li>
<li><strong>Cross-platform</strong> - runs natively on macOS, Windows, and Linux</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Privacy-First Architecture</strong></h3><a id="user-content-privacy-first-architecture" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Privacy-First Architecture" href="#privacy-first-architecture"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Unlike cloud-based solutions, Pluely keeps everything local:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Your data never touches any servers</strong> - all processing happens locally and with your LLM provider</li>
<li><strong>API keys stored securely</strong> in your browser's localStorage</li>
<li><strong>No telemetry or tracking</strong> - your conversations stay private, not stored anywhere</li>
<li><strong>Offline-first design</strong> - works without internet (except for AI API calls)</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Build for Production</h3><a id="user-content-build-for-production" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Build for Production" href="#build-for-production"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Build the application
npm run tauri build"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Build the application</span>

<p dir="auto">This creates platform-specific installers in <code>src-tauri/target/release/bundle/</code>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>macOS</strong>: <code>.dmg</code></li>
<li><strong>Windows</strong>: <code>.msi</code>, <code>.exe</code></li>
<li><strong>Linux</strong>: <code>.deb</code>, <code>.rpm</code>, <code>.AppImage</code></li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Security &amp; Privacy</h2><a id="user-content-security--privacy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Security &amp; Privacy" href="#security--privacy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Local API Key Storage</strong></h3><a id="user-content-local-api-key-storage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Local API Key Storage" href="#local-api-key-storage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>API keys are stored in <strong>browser localStorage</strong> (not sent to any server)</li>
<li><strong>No telemetry</strong> - your keys never leave your device</li>
<li><strong>Session-based</strong> - keys can be cleared anytime</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Secure API Communication</strong></h3><a id="user-content-secure-api-communication" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Secure API Communication" href="#secure-api-communication"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Direct HTTPS</strong> connections to AI providers</li>
<li><strong>No proxy servers</strong> - your requests go straight to the AI service</li>
<li><strong>Request signing</strong> handled locally</li>
<li><strong>TLS encryption</strong> for all API communications</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Data Handling</strong></h3><a id="user-content-data-handling" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Data Handling" href="#data-handling"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>No conversation logging</strong> - messages aren't stored anywhere</li>
<li><strong>Temporary session data</strong> - cleared on app restart</li>
<li><strong>Local file processing</strong> - images processed in-browser</li>
<li><strong>No analytics</strong> - completely private usage</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Why Frontend API Calls Are Better</strong></h3><a id="user-content-why-frontend-api-calls-are-better" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why Frontend API Calls Are Better" href="#why-frontend-api-calls-are-better"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Pluely makes API calls directly from your frontend because:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>🔒 Maximum Privacy</strong>: Your conversations never touch our servers</li>
<li><strong>🚀 Better Performance</strong>: Direct connection = faster responses</li>
<li><strong>📱 Always Local</strong>: Your data stays on your device, always</li>
<li><strong>🔍 Transparent</strong>: You can inspect every network request in dev tools</li>
<li><strong>⚡ No Bottlenecks</strong>: No server capacity limits or downtime</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Performance Optimizations</h2><a id="user-content-performance-optimizations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Performance Optimizations" href="#performance-optimizations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Tauri Advantages</strong></h3><a id="user-content-tauri-advantages" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tauri Advantages" href="#tauri-advantages"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Native binary</strong> - no JavaScript runtime overhead</li>
<li><strong>Rust backend</strong> - memory-safe, ultra-fast</li>
<li><strong>Small bundle size</strong> - ~10MB total app size</li>
<li><strong>Instant startup</strong> - launches in &lt;100ms</li>
<li><strong>Low memory usage</strong> - typically &lt;50MB RAM</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Frontend Optimizations</strong></h3><a id="user-content-frontend-optimizations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Frontend Optimizations" href="#frontend-optimizations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>React 18</strong> with concurrent features</li>
<li><strong>TypeScript</strong> for compile-time optimization</li>
<li><strong>Vite</strong> for lightning-fast development</li>
<li><strong>Tree shaking</strong> - only bundle used code</li>
<li><strong>Lazy loading</strong> - components load on demand</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Development</h2><a id="user-content-development" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Development" href="#development"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Architecture Overview</h3><a id="user-content-architecture-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Architecture Overview" href="#architecture-overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Frontend (React + TypeScript + Tauri)</h4><a id="user-content-frontend-react--typescript--tauri" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Frontend (React + TypeScript + Tauri)" href="#frontend-react--typescript--tauri"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Contribution Guidelines</strong></h3><a id="user-content-contribution-guidelines" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Contribution Guidelines" href="#contribution-guidelines"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>🚀 Only fixes and feature PRs are welcome.</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>❌ Please do NOT submit pull requests that:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Adding new AI providers</li>
<li>Adding new speech-to-text providers</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>✅ What we DO welcome:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Bug fixes and performance improvements</li>
<li>Feature improvements to existing functionality</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Contributing Guidelines</strong></h3><a id="user-content-contributing-guidelines" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Contributing Guidelines" href="#contributing-guidelines"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Fork</strong> the repository</li>
<li><strong>Create</strong> a feature branch (<code>git checkout -b feature/amazing-feature</code>)</li>
<li><strong>Commit</strong> your changes (<code>git commit -m 'Add amazing feature'</code>)</li>
<li><strong>Push</strong> to the branch (<code>git push origin feature/amazing-feature</code>)</li>
<li><strong>Open</strong> a Pull Request</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Code Style</strong></h3><a id="user-content-code-style" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Code Style" href="#code-style"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

  <h2 class="mb-3 h4">About</h2>

      <p class="f4 my-3">
        The Open Source Alternative to Cluely - A lightning-fast, privacy-first AI assistant that works seamlessly during meetings, interviews, and conversations without anyone knowing. Built with Tauri for native performance, just 10MB. Completely undetectable in video calls, screen shares, and recordings.
      </p>
      <div class="my-3 d-flex flex-items-center">
